bc_cheatinterface_button_effect = {
    potential = { always = yes }
    allow = { always = yes }
}

bc_cheatinterface_button_title = {
    potential = { always = no }
    allow = { always = no }
}

############################# Resource Minerals #################################
bc_cheatinterface_button_resource_minerals = {
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {
        is_ai = no
    }
    effect = {
        country_event = {
            id = "bccheatinterface.1001"
        }
    }
}

bc_cheatinterface_button_resource_minerals_t1 = {
    potential = {
        always = yes
    }
    allow = {
        is_ai = no
    }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t1_modifier
                has_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t1
            }
            remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t1_modifier
            remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t1
        }
        else = {
            add_modifier = {
                modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t1
                days = -1
            }
            hidden_effect = {
                set_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t1_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t2_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t3_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t4_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t5_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t6_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t7_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t8_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t9_modifier
                remove_country_flag = bc_has_resource_minerals_t10_modifier
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t2
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t3
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t4
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t5
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t6
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t7
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t8
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t9
                remove_modifier = bc_resource_minerals_t10
            }
        }
    }
}

        always = yes

        is_ai = no
    }
